Boot Chain:
  UEFI -> BOOTX64.EFI (SUSE shim, Microsoft-signed)
       -> grub.efi (Custom GRUB stub, MOK-signed, NO shim_lock)
       -> GRUB Menu (5 sec timeout):
          1. Install (Custom MOK) - For Physical Hardware
          2. Install (VMware Original) - For VMware VMs
          3. MokManager - Enroll/Delete MOK keys
          4. Reboot into UEFI Firmware Settings
          5-6. Reboot/Shutdown

First Boot Instructions:
  1. Boot from USB with UEFI Secure Boot ENABLED
  2. You should see a BLUE MokManager screen (shim's)
     [33mNOTE:[0m If you see your laptop's security dialog instead,
           check that CSM/Legacy boot is DISABLED in BIOS.
  3. Select 'Enroll key from disk'
  4. Navigate to USB root -> ENROLL_THIS_KEY_IN_MOKMANAGER.cer
     (This is YOUR MOK certificate: CN=HABv4 Secure Boot MOK)
  5. Confirm and select REBOOT (not continue)
  6. After reboot, GRUB Menu appears (5 sec timeout)
  7. Select installation option:
     - 'Install (Custom MOK)' for PHYSICAL hardware with Secure Boot
     - 'Install (VMware Original)' for VMware virtual machines
  8. Follow the interactive installer prompts
     (Disk, hostname, password are configurable; packages are preset)

  - Create dongle with: PhotonOS-HABv4Emulation-ISOCreator -u /dev/sdX
